the below program to evolve a system S that discovers profitable trading strategies for BTC directional prediction on a 15-minute horizon.\n\n## Primary Objective\n\nBuild and continuously improve a trading system that predicts whether **BTC will go UP or DOWN over the next 15 minutes**.\n\nThe task is strictly:\n\n- **Asset:** BTC\n\n- **Prediction type:** binary directional classification (**UP / DOWN**)\n\n- **Forecast horizon:** **15 minutes**\n\n- **Trading style:** high-frequency directional decision making\n\n- **Primary success metric:** **directional accuracy >= 65%**\n\n- **Secondary success metric:** **more than 90 bets per month**\n\nThe system must optimize for both:\n\n1. **Prediction quality**: at least **65% directional accuracy**\n\n2. **Trading activity**: at least **90 valid bets per month**\n\nA model that is accurate but generates too few trades is not acceptable.  \n\nA model that generates many trades but fails to reach 65% directional accuracy is also not acceptable.\n\n---\n\n## Initial State (build first)\n\nS₀ = online continuous adaptive trading system which:\n\n- uses **online market data** for training and updating\n\n- uses **evolutionary model search** (mutation, crossover, replacement of weak models)\n\n- uses **strict walk-forward validation**\n\n- uses **online Sharpe filtering**\n\n- uses **horizon ensembles** H = {1h, 4h, 8h, 12h, 24h} as contextual signals\n\n- uses **consensus gating** for signal generation\n\n- uses **time-series foundation models** and sequence models\n\n- is centered on the **main execution target = BTC up/down over the next 15 minutes**\n\n---\n\n## Core Prediction Task\n\nAt each decision point, the system must output one of:\n\n- **UP** = BTC is expected to be higher in 15 minutes\n\n- **DOWN** = BTC is expected to be lower in 15 minutes\n\n- optional: **NO TRADE** only if confidence is too low\n\nThe system should be designed to maximize profitable directional decisions while maintaining enough signal frequency to exceed **90 bets per month**.\n\n---\n\n## Optimization Targets\n\nThe system must optimize for the following target profile:\n\n- **Directional accuracy >= 65%**\n\n- **Bets per month > 90**\n\n- **Positive net profitability**\n\n- **Strong Sharpe ratio**\n\n- **Controlled drawdown**\n\n- **Robustness across market regimes**\n\n- **Stable out-of-sample performance**\n\n---\n\n## Fitness Priorities\n\nFitness should prioritize:\n\n1. **Directional accuracy on 15m BTC prediction**\n\n2. **Monthly bet count**\n\n3. **PnL**\n\n4. **Sharpe ratio**\n\n5. **Drawdown control**\n\n6. **Regime robustness**\n\n7. **Consistency across walk-forward folds**\n\nAny candidate that fails either:\n\n- **accuracy < 65%**\n\n- **bets/month <= 90**\n\nshould be considered below target even if other metrics look good.\n\n---\n\n## Data and Modeling Requirements\n\nThe system should:\n\n- learn from **BTC market structure**\n\n- exploit **short-term directional patterns**\n\n- use **multi-timescale context** while keeping the target fixed at 15m\n\n- adapt online as conditions change\n\n- discover alpha from:\n\n  - price action\n\n  - volatility\n\n  - momentum\n\n  - order-flow proxies\n\n  - volume\n\n  - derivatives context if available\n\n  - regime features\n\n  - cross-horizon agreement\n\nLonger horizons {1h, 4h, 8h, 12h, 24h} should be used as **contextual ensemble inputs**, not as replacements for the core 15m target.\n\n---\n\n## Validation Rules\n\nThe system must use:\n\n- strict **temporal splits**\n\n- strict **walk-forward validation**\n\n- no lookahead bias\n\n- no leakage\n\n- no random split for final evaluation\n\n- evaluation on realistic trading frequency\n\n- explicit measurement of:\n\n  - accuracy\n\n  - number of bets\n\n  - PnL\n\n  - Sharpe\n\n  - drawdown\n\n  - regime-specific performance\n\nA candidate is only truly good if it remains strong in out-of-sample walk-forward testing.\n\n---\n\n## Evolution Strategy\n\nRun this loop continuously:\n\nloop t = 1..∞\n\n    S_t = design_or_modify(S_{t-1})   # implement the current design\n\n    O_t = run(S_t)                    # train, validate, and trade / paper trade\n\n    P_t = measure(O_t)                # evaluate accuracy, bets/month, Sharpe, PnL, drawdown, regime behavior\n\n    Δ_t = reflect(S_t, P_t)           # identify weaknesses and bottlenecks\n\n    S_{t+1} = improve(S_t, Δ_t)       # produce a better design\n\nend\n\n---\n\n## Reflection Requirements\n\nDuring reflection, explicitly diagnose:\n\n- why accuracy is below 65% if target is missed\n\n- why signal frequency is below 90 bets/month if target is missed\n\n- whether the consensus gate is too strict\n\n- whether the model is overfitting to specific regimes\n\n- whether the ensemble is improving or diluting edge\n\n- whether the system is sacrificing too much frequency for precision\n\n- whether the system is producing too many low-quality trades\n\n- whether thresholding should be tightened or loosened\n\nThe next design must directly address the identified weakness.\n\n---\n\n## Design Guidance\n\nThe system should search At least MIN_MODELS_AGREE models must agree on direction\n    - Average confidence must exceed MIN_CONFIDENCE\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        min_models_agree: int = ConsensusConfig.MIN_MODELS_AGREE,\n        min_confidence: float = ConsensusConfig.MIN_CONFIDENCE\n    ):\n        self.min_models_agree = min_models_agree\n        self.min_confidence = min_confidence\n\n    def decide(\n        self,\n        models: List[Individual],\n        X: pd.DataFrame\n    ) -> pd.Series:\n        \"\"\"\n        Generate final trading signals (UP=1, DOWN=0, NO_TRADE=-1).\n\n        Args:\n            models: list of trained model individuals\n            X: feature DataFrame to predict on\n\n        Returns:\n            Series of signals (1, 0, or -1) aligned to X.index\n        \"\"\"\n        signals = pd.Series(index=X.index, data=0)\n        probas_matrix = []\n\n        for ind in models:\n            try:\n                proba = ind.model.predict_proba(X)\n                probas_matrix.append(proba)\n            except Exception as e:\n                continue\n\n        if not probas_matrix:\n            # No model worked, all NO_TRADE\n            signals[:] = -1\n            return signals\n\n        probas_array = np.array(probas_matrix)  # shape: (n_models, n_samples)\n\n        # Average confidence for each sample\n        avg_proba = probas_array.mean(axis=0)\n\n        # Count models predicting UP\n        up_votes = (probas_array >= 0.5).sum(axis=0)\n\n        down_votes = len(probas_matrix) - up_votes\n\n        # Apply gating rules\n        for i, (avg_p, up, down) in enumerate(zip(avg_proba, up_votes, down_votes)):\n            # Check agreement\n            if up >= self.min_models_agree:\n                direction = 1\n                confidence = avg_p\n            elif down >= self.min_models_agree:\n                direction = 0\n                confidence = 1 - avg_p  # confidence in DOWN is 1 - avg_proba\n            else:\n                signals.iloc[i] = -1\n                continue\n\n            # Check confidence threshold\n            if confidence >= self.min_confidence:\n                signals.iloc[i] = direction\n            else:\n                signals.iloc[i] = -1\n\n        return signals\n\n    def adjust_thresholds(\n        self,\n        recent_performance: Dict[str, float],\n        target_sharpe: float = 1.0,\n        target_profit_factor: float = 1.2,\n        target_accuracy: float = 0.65,\n        target_bets: float = 90.0\n    ):\n        \"\"\"\n        Dynamically adjust consensus thresholds based on recent performance.\n\n        Prioritizes risk-adjusted returns (Sharpe) and profitability (profit factor).\n        If Sharpe or profit factor are below target, tighten thresholds to improve quality.\n        If accuracy is high but Sharpe is low, also tighten (filter out low-quality trades).\n        If bets are too low and accuracy acceptable, loosen to increase frequency.\n        \"\"\"\n        sharpe = recent_performance.get(\"sharpe\", -1000.0)\n        profit_factor = recent_performance.get(\"profit_factor\", 0.0)\n        accuracy = recent_performance.get(\"accuracy\", 0.5)\n        bets_per_month = recent_performance.get(\"bets_per_month\", 0.0)\n\n        # If extremely few trades (or none), loosen to generate activity\n        if bets_per_month < 30.0:\n            self.min_confidence = max(0.5, self.min_confidence - 0.05)\n            self.min_models_agree = max(1, self.min_models_agree - 1)\n            # After loosening for low activity, skip further adjustments this cycle\n            self.min_models_agree = max(1, min(5, self.min_models_agree))\n            self.min_confidence = max(0.5, min(0.95, self.min_confidence))\n            return\n\n        # Primary: Sharpe and profitability\n        if sharpe < target_sharpe or profit_factor < target_profit_factor:\n            # Poor risk-adjusted/absolute performance: tighten to filter trades\n            self.min_confidence = min(0.9, self.min_confidence + 0.05)\n            self.min_models_agree = min(5, self.min_models_agree + 1)\n        elif accuracy < target_accuracy:\n            # Directional accuracy insufficient: tighten to require stronger agreement\n            self.min_confidence = min(0.9, self.min_confidence + 0.03)\n        elif bets_per_month < target_bets and accuracy >= target_accuracy:\n            # Too few trades despite decent accuracy: loosen thresholds\n            self.min_confidence = max(0.5, self.min_confidence - 0.02)\n            self.min_models_agree = max(1, self.min_models_agree - 1)\n        # else: keep thresholds stable\n\n        # Clamp to reasonable ranges\n        self.min_models_agree = max(1, min(5, self.min_models_agree))\n        self.min_confidence = max(0.5, min(0.95, self.min_confidence))\n\n    def get_params(self) -> dict:\n        return {\n            \"min_models_agree\": self.min_models_agree,\n            \"min_confidence\": self.min_confidence\n        }\n","numLines":143,"startLine":1,"totalLines":143}}}

The Claude API returns streaming events; the code collects the final result_text from the \"result\" event. That result_text should be the entire conversation? Actually the code in `_run_claude_once` processes events and accumulates `result_text` from events of type \"result\". At the end, it returns result_text as the overall result (the assistant's final message). So the rollout is the final message from the assistant, not the full transcript. The full transcript (including tool calls) might be in the raw lines but they are not included in the result. The code then writes `rollout_text` as the extracted text from result (which is just the final assistant message). So the rollout file does NOT contain tool call details. But there is also an `output.txt` file written in the run_dir, which contains the raw JSON lines from the subprocess. That would contain the full transcript including tool calls.\n\nWe saw that the `output.txt` is missing in the incomplete steps. In completed steps, there should be an output.txt. Wait, entry_cost + exit_cost = 0.001 + 0.0005? Actually fee_rate=0.001 (0.1%) and slippage=0.0005 (0.05%) each side? The simulator uses entry_cost + exit_cost for roundturn. For a long: entry = price*(1+entry_cost) where entry_cost = fee_rate+slippage = 0.0015. exit = next_close*(1-exit_cost) where exit_cost = fee_rate+slippage = 0.0015. So total cost effect is approximately (1+0.0015)*(1-0.0015) ≈ 1 - 0.0015^2 ≈ 0.99999775, essentially a cost of about 0.0015 relative to price? Actually net effect on return: return = (exit_price/entry)-1 ≈ (next_close*(1-0.0015) / (current_price*(1+0.0015))) -1 ≈ (next_close/current_price)*(1 - 0.003) -1. Approximately, the cost reduces gross return by ~0.3% (because both sides). That is significant. Indeed, if gross return is +0.2%, after ~0.3% cost it's -0.1%. So to be net positive, gross win must exceed 0.3% to overcome costs, assuming no loss bigger. Our average gross win is 0.067%, far below costs. So most winning trades are actually net losers after costs! That could explain why profit factor is low despite high accuracy: the model's predictions are directionally correct but the magnitude of price movement is insufficient to cover transaction costs. So the system is essentially paying more in fees/slippage than it gains from small moves.\n\nThus the root cause is that the model's predictions are correct in direction but not strong enough to generate sufficient magnitude to overcome costs. This is a classic case of a high win rate but negative expectancy due to small wins and large losses (or here, small wins net negative after costs, losses bigger net negative).\n\nSolutions:\n- Reduce transaction costs: lower fee rate? Can't, fees are fixed. Reduce slippage via better execution? Not in simulation.\n- Increase average win magnitude: This could be done by only taking trades where the predicted magnitude is high (i.e., use a confidence threshold that correlates with expected move size). Our current confidence threshold is 0.68 (and models_agree=2). Lowering confidence threshold might include trades with weaker conviction, which might have even smaller average moves? Not sure. Possibly higher confidence corresponds to stronger predicted moves. If confidence is high, maybe the expected move is larger. But we already have high confidence threshold. Actually it's the opposite: we require high confidence, which might select trades where the model is very sure, but that could be in low volatility regimes where moves are small. Lowering confidence might include more volatile regimes with larger moves. We need to test.\n\n- Increase bet size? That would scale both gains and losses proportionally, so profit factor unchanged. However, if we cannot increase average win, scaling up would just increase volatility but not improve Sharpe.\n\n- Use a take-profit to lock in gains and let losses run? That's opposite of typical; we have stop-loss but no take-profit. Letting winners run could increase average win, but we have fixed 15-minute holding. Could extend holding period? Not according to the 15-minute horizon requirement. The target is 15-minute directional. So exit is forced at next candle.\n\n- Perhaps the model is not capturing the magnitude, only direction. Not necessarily.\n\n- Could adjust position sizing based on confidence: if confidence is high, bet larger; if low, bet smaller. later)\n                    ind.fitness = accuracy\n                    print(f\"      -> fitness={ind.fitness:.4f}\", flush=True)\n                except Exception as e:\n     Run walk-forward validation with a single temporal split.\n        Train on data before the validation period, test on the most recent validation period.\n        This provides an honest OOS performance estimate without leakage.\n        \"\"\"\n        print(\"Running walk-forward validation (single split)...\", flush=True)\n\n        df_sorted = df_sorted.iloc[-val_rows:].copy()\n        train_df = df_sorted.iloc[:-val_rows].copy()\n\n        # Prepare OHLC data for simulation with stop-loss\n        valid_ohlc = valid_df[['close', 'high', y_valid = valid_df[\"target\"]\n\n        # Evolve a fresh population on the training set\n        pop = Population(\n            population_size=ModelConfig.POPULATION_SIZE,\n            model_types=ModelConfig.MODEL_TYPES,\n            mutation_rate=ModelConfig.MUTATION_RATE,\n            crossover_rate=ModelConfig.CROSSOVER_RATE,\n            elitism_count=ModelConfig.ELITISM_COUNT\n        )\n        pop.initialize(input_dim=X_train.shape[1], feature_names=self.feature_names)\n\n        for gen in          for ind in pop.individuals:\n                try:\n                    ind.model.fit(X_train, y_train)\n                    # Use training accuracy as fitness for selection\n                    pred = ind.model.predict(X_train, threshold=0.5)\n                    ind.fitness = (pred == y_train).mean()\n                except Exception as e:\n                    print(f\"    Training error: individual {i+1}/{len(pop.individuals)} (failed training)\", flush=True)\n                continue\n            try:\n                print(f\"  Rescoring individual {i+1}/{len(pop.individuals)} ({ind.model_type})\", flush=True)\n                # Predict on validation\n                pred_valid = ind.model.predict(X_valid, threshold=0.5)\n                # Ensure pred_valid is a Series with ind.validation_metrics = v_metrics\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"  Validation rescoring error: {e}\", flush=True)\n                ind.fitness = -1000.0\n\n        # At least MIN_MODELS_AGREE models must agree on direction\n    - Average confidence must exceed MIN_CONFIDENCE\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        min_models_agree: int = ConsensusConfig.MIN_MODELS_AGREE,\n        min_confidence: float = ConsensusConfig.MIN_CONFIDENCE\n    ):\n        self.min_models_agree = min_models_agree\n        self.min_confidence = min_confidence\n\n    def decide(\n        self,\n        models: List[Individual],\n        X: pd.DataFrame\n    ) -> pd.Series:\n        \"\"\"\n        Generate final trading signals (UP=1, DOWN=0, NO_TRADE=-1).\n\n        Args:\n            models: list of trained model individuals\n            X: feature DataFrame to predict on\n\n        Returns:\n            Series of signals (1, 0, or -1) aligned to X.index\n        \"\"\"\n        signals = pd.Series(index=X.index, data=0)\n        probas_matrix = []\n\n        for ind in models:\n            try:\n                proba = ind.model.predict_proba(X)\n                probas_matrix.append(proba)\n            except Exception as e:\n                continue\n\n        if not probas_matrix:\n            # No model worked, all NO_TRADE\n            signals[:] = -1\n            return signals\n\n        probas_array = np.array(probas_matrix)  # shape: (n_models, n_samples)\n\n        # Average confidence for each sample\n        avg_proba = probas_array.mean(axis=0)\n\n        # Count models predicting UP\n        up_votes = (probas_array >= 0.5).sum(axis=0)\n\n        down_votes = len(probas_matrix) - up_votes\n\n        # Apply gating rules\n        for i, (avg_p, up, down) in enumerate(zip(avg_proba, up_votes, down_votes)):\n            # Check agreement\n            if up >= self.min_models_agree:\n                direction = 1\n                confidence = avg_p\n            elif down >= self.min_models_agree:\n                direction = 0\n                confidence = 1 - avg_p  # confidence in DOWN is 1 - avg_proba\n            else:\n                signals.iloc[i] = -1\n                continue\n\n            # Check confidence threshold\n            if confidence >= self.min_confidence:\n                signals.iloc[i] = direction\n            else:\n                signals.iloc[i] = -1\n\n        return signals\n\n    def adjust_thresholds(\n        self,\n        recent_performance: Dict[str, float],\n        target_sharpe: float = 1.0,\n        target_profit_factor: float = 1.2,\n        target_accuracy: float = 0.65,\n        target_bets: float = 90.0\n    ):\n        \"\"\"\n        Dynamically adjust consensus thresholds based on recent performance.\n\n        Prioritizes risk-adjusted returns (Sharpe) and profitability (profit factor).\n        If Sharpe or profit factor are below target, tighten thresholds to improve quality.\n        If accuracy is high but Sharpe is low, also tighten (filter out low-quality trades).\n        If bets are too low and accuracy acceptable, loosen to increase frequency.\n        \"\"\"\n        sharpe = recent_performance.get(\"sharpe\", -1000.0)\n        profit_factor = recent_performance.get(\"profit_factor\", 0.0)\n        accuracy = recent_performance.get(\"accuracy\", 0.5)\n        bets_per_month = recent_performance.get(\"bets_per_month\", 0.0)\n\n        # If extremely few trades (or none), loosen to generate activity\n        if bets_per_month < 30.0:\n            self.min_confidence = max(0.5, self.min_confidence - 0.05)\n            self.min_models_agree = max(1, self.min_models_agree - 1)\n            # After loosening for low activity, skip further adjustments this cycle\n            self.min_models_agree = max(1, min(5, self.min_models_agree))\n            self.min_confidence = max(0.5, min(0.95, self.min_confidence))\n            return\n\n        # Primary: Sharpe and profitability\n        if sharpe < target_sharpe or profit_factor < target_profit_factor:\n            # Poor risk-adjusted/absolute performance: tighten to filter trades\n            self.min_confidence = min(0.9, self.min_confidence + 0.05)\n            self.min_models_agree = min(5, self.min_models_agree + 1)\n        elif accuracy < target_accuracy:\n            # Directional accuracy insufficient: tighten to require stronger agreement\n            self.min_confidence = min(0.9, self.min_confidence + 0.03)\n        elif bets_per_month < target_bets and accuracy >= target_accuracy:\n            # Too few trades despite decent accuracy: loosen thresholds\n            self.min_confidence = max(0.5, self.min_confidence - 0.02)\n            self.min_models_agree = max(1, self.min_models_agree - 1)\n        # else: keep thresholds stable\n\n        # Clamp to reasonable ranges\n        self.min_models_agree = max(1, min(5, self.min_models_agree))\n        self.min_confidence = max(0.5, min(0.95, self.min_confidence))\n\n    def get_params(self) -> dict:\n        return {\n            \"min_models_agree\": self.min_models_agree,\n            \"min_confidence\": self.min_confidence\n        }\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":108,"oldLines":6,"newStart":108,"newLines":12,"lines":["         accuracy = recent_performance.get(\"accuracy\", 0.5)","         bets_per_month = recent_performance.get(\"bets_per_month\", 0.0)"," ","+        # If we already have sufficient accuracy and activity, avoid tightening thresholds","+        # which could zero out trading.
